    SELECT [t2].[Name], [t0].[TagId], [t0].[TaskId], [t2].[Id]
    FROM [TaskTags] AS [t0]

    SELECT [p0].[ProjectId], [p0].[UserId], [a0].[Id], [a0].[AccessFailedCount], [a0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a0].[Email], [a0].[EmailConfirmed], [a0].[FirstName], [a0].[LastName], [a0].[LockoutEnabled], [a0].[LockoutEnd], [a0].[NormalizedEmail], [a0].[NormalizedUserName], [a0].[PasswordHash], [a0].[PhoneNumber], [a0].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a0].[SecurityStamp], [a0].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a0].[UserName]
